### Creating New England

country_event = { # Player America gets a choice to swap to New England
	id = new_england_events.1
	title = new_england_events.1.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.1.d.usa
		trigger = { tag = USA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.1.d.wca
		trigger = { tag = WCA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.1.d.ACC
		trigger = { tag = ACC }
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.1.d.APG
		trigger = { tag = APG }
	}

	trigger = { is_ai = no }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We will deal with this later
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.1 option new_england_events.1.a"
		name = new_england_events.1.a
	}

	option = { # Switch to New England
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.1 option new_england_events.1.b"
		name = new_england_events.1.b
		hidden_effect = { USA_emergency_recruitment_fix = yes }
		NEE = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

country_event = { # ACW nation informed that Canada has seized New England
	id = new_england_events.2
	title = new_england_events.2.t
	desc = new_england_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		is_american_tag = yes
	}

	option = { # We will deal with this later
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.2 option new_england_events.2.a"
		name = new_england_events.2.a
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = ACW_occupied_new_england }
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada doesn't occupy New England
	id = new_england_events.3
	title = new_england_events.3.t
	desc = new_england_events.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = WCA
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.3 option new_england_events.3.a"
		name = new_england_events.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_new_england_units
		NEE_move_generals = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			create_USA_garrison_template = yes
			932 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Massachusetts Coastal Defense Force\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.6"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 6732 #Boston
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Massachusetts National Guard\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.6"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 6732 #Boston
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"North-Eastern Department Reserve Force\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 6732 #Boston
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
			}
			933 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Vermont National Guard\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 4445 #Montpelier
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
			}
			932 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Rhode Island National Guard\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 9832 #Providence
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada Debates Question of New England
	id = new_england_events.5
	title = new_england_events.5.t
	desc = new_england_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.5 option new_england_events.5.a"
		name = new_england_events.5.a #Set up the provisional government
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_WCA }
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = DEFAULT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA_spawn_new_england = yes
		NEE = {
			NEE_Starting_Great_Depression_Effect = yes
		}
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;NEE SPAWNED"
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.5 option new_england_events.5.b"
		name = new_england_events.5.b #Set up the provisional government (play as New England)
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		USA_spawn_new_england = yes
		NEE = {
			NEE_Starting_Great_Depression_Effect = yes
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;NEE SPAWNED"
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.5 option new_england_events.5.c"
		name = new_england_events.5.c #Continue with the military occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_liberal_government = yes
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_WCA }
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = DEFAULT }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_new_england = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			add_compliance = -25
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		set_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.80 days = 25 random_days = 10 }
			CAN = { USA_create_virginia_hall_operative = yes }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Independent New England
	id = new_england_events.6
	title = new_england_events.6.t
	desc = new_england_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.6 option new_england_events.6.a"
		name = new_england_events.6.a
		add_political_power = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.216 days = 90 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.54 days = 200 random_days = 100 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.64 days = 1100 } #This should probably get moved to the USA history file later so a more concrete date may be set.
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.59 days = 600 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.68 days = 60 random_days = 15 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.151 days = 400 random_days = 45 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.153 days = 245 random_days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.159 days = 353 }
			### Firing the flavour events
			NEE_Flavour_Events = yes
		}
	}
}

### Independence ###

country_event = { # New England requests home rule
	id = new_england_events.12
	title = new_england_events.12.t
	desc = new_england_events.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NEE = {
			is_subject_of = CAN
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.12 option new_england_events.12.a"
		name = new_england_events.12.a #give them home rule
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = var:NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 250
				NEE = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_more_likely_independent
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NEE = {
					has_country_flag = less_likely_independence
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NEE
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			clr_country_flag = NEE_more_likely_independent
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.13 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.12 option new_england_events.12.b"
		name = new_england_events.12.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NEE = { USA_has_america_cosmetic_tag = yes }
					strength_ratio = { tag = NEE ratio < 1.0 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 80 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 90 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy = 100 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		NEE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.14 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England granted home rule
	id = new_england_events.13
	title = new_england_events.13.t
	desc = new_england_events.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject_of = CAN
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.13 option new_england_events.13.a"
		name = new_england_events.13.a
		add_political_power = 50
		overlord = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NEE
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused home rule
	id = new_england_events.14
	title = new_england_events.14.t
	desc = new_england_events.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	}

	}
}

country_event = { # Declaration of Independence
	id = new_england_events.15
	title = new_england_events.15.t
	desc = new_england_events.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.15 option new_england_events.15.a"
		name = new_england_events.15.a #We're fine with it
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = -100
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.15 option new_england_events.15.b"
		name = new_england_events.15.b #How dare they!
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					NOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = NEE
						ratio < 1.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England Hurricane
	id = new_england_events.40
	title = new_england_events.40.t
	desc = new_england_events.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_hurricane

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			controls_state = 357
			controls_state = 358
			controls_state = 359
			controls_state = 796
			controls_state = 930
			controls_state = 931
			controls_state = 932
			controls_state = 933
			controls_state = 934
			controls_state = 935
		}
	}

	option = { # Oh the Humanity
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.40 option new_england_events.40.a"
		name = new_england_events.40.a
		add_manpower = -700
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					controls_state = 935
					controls_state = 931
					controls_state = 932
					controls_state = 933
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					if = {
						limit = { controls_state = 935 }
						935 = {
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = dockyard level > 0.9 } }
								damage_building = { type = dockyard damage = 0.9 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { naval_base > 0 } #non_damaged_building_level doesn't support provincial buildings
								damage_building = { type = naval_base damage = 0.9 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = infrastructure level > 0.7 } }
								damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 0.7 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = industrial_complex level > 0.25 } }
								damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 0.25 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = arms_factory level > 0.15 } }
								damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 0.15 }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { controls_state = 931 }
						931 = {
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = dockyard level > 0.4 } }
								damage_building = { type = dockyard damage = 0.4 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { naval_base > 0 } #non_damaged_building_level doesn't support provincial buildings
								damage_building = { type = naval_base damage = 0.4 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = infrastructure level > 0.5 } }
								damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 0.5 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = industrial_complex level > 0.25 } }
								damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 0.25 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = arms_factory level > 0.1 } }
								damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 0.1 }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { controls_state = 932 }
						932 = {
							if = {
								limit = { non_damaged_building_level = { building = infrastructure level > 0.5 } }

							}
						}

country_event = { # Creation of the Railroad
	id = new_england_events.50
	title = new_england_events.50.t
	desc = new_england_events.50.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We can only do so much!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.50 option new_england_events.50.a"
		name = new_england_events.50.a
		add_political_power = 30
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { #WCA Refugees
				limit = {
					country_exists = WCA
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_wca_times
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_wca_manpower
					value = 2984
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_wca_guns
					value = 236
				}
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.51 days = 14 random_days = 7 } #Erie lake
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.55 days = 60 random_days = 7 } #Monthly intake refugees
			}
			if = { #APG Refugees
				limit = {
					country_exists = APG
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_apg_times
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_apg_manpower
					value = 2680
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_apg_guns
					value = 169
				}
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.56 days = 60 random_days = 7 } #Monthly intake refugees
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = new_england_events.51

	desc = new_england_events.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_great_migration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = WCA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = WCA
		}
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	option = { # Send covert agents to assist the process
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.51 option new_england_events.51.a"
		name = new_england_events.51.a

			}
		}

	}
}

country_event = { # Successful Smuggling action in the Great Lakes Region (Underground Railroad)
	id = new_england_events.52
	title = new_england_events.52.t
	desc = new_england_events.52.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_great_migration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = WCA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = WCA
		}
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			multiply_variable = {
				var = NEE_ugr_wca_manpower
				value = 1.1
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = NEE_ugr_wca_guns
				value = 1.1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # The Resistance grows Stronger!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.52 option new_england_events.52.a"
		name = new_england_events.52.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_ugr_wca_10p_increase
		add_manpower = 13789
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 756
			producer = WCA
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			amount = 23
			producer = WCA
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		random_list = {
			66 = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.52 days = 25 random_days = 7 }
			}
			34 = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.53 days = 8 random_days = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Operation Pointblank
	id = new_england_events.76
	title = new_england_events.76.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.76.d.nee #NEE sends the raid
		trigger = {
			tag = NEE
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.76.d.defender #Receiving bombardment
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = NEE }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_bombing_run

	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { tag = NEE }
			has_country_flag = NEE_prepared_pointblank
			OR = {
				has_war_with = 261.controller #Ohio
				has_war_with = 393.controller #Michigan
				has_war_with = 395.controller #Illinois
				has_war_with = 396.controller #Indiana
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = NEE }
				clr_country_flag = NEE_prepared_pointblank
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = large_plane_airframe amount = -27 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = 261.controller }
					261 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.5 } } #Ohio
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = 393.controller }
					393 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.2 } } #Michigan
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = 395.controller }
					395 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.8 } } #Illinois
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = 396.controller }
					396 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.3 } } #Indiana
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							controls_state = 261 #Ohio
							controls_state = 393 #Michigan
							controls_state = 395 #Illinois
							controls_state = 396 #Indiana
						}
					}
					country_event = new_england_events.76
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.76 option new_england_events.76.a"
		name = new_england_events.76.a
		trigger = {
			tag = NEE
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = large_plane_airframe amount = -27 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = 261.controller }
				261 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.5 } } #Ohio
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = 393.controller }
				393 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.2 } } #Michigan
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = 395.controller }
				395 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.8 } } #Illinois
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = 396.controller }
				396 = { damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 1.3 } } #Indiana
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.76 option new_england_events.76.b"
		name = new_england_events.76.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = NEE }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {

# Weapon Designer Choice
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.77
	title = new_england_events.77.t
	desc = new_england_events.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rifles

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.77 option new_england_events.77.a"
		name = new_england_events.77.a # Springfield Armory
		ai_chance = { base = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
			if = {
				limit = { amount_taken_ideas = { amount > 0 slots = { materiel_manufacturer } } }
				add_ideas = USA_springfield_armory
			}
			else = {
				army_experience = 15
			}
		}
		else = {
			mio:USA_springfield_armory_organisation = {
				add_mio_size = 1
				add_mio_funds = 500
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.77 option new_england_events.77.b"
		name = new_england_events.77.b # Winchester
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
			if = {
				limit = { amount_taken_ideas = { amount > 0 slots = { materiel_manufacturer } } }
				add_ideas = USA_winchester_repeating_arms
			}
			else = {
				army_experience = 15
			}
		}
		else = {
			mio:USA_winchester_repeating_arms_organisation = {
				add_mio_size = 1
				add_mio_funds = 500
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons }
			}
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_add_tech_detailed
					NAME = country_culture|infantry_equipment_2
					TECH = infantry_equipment_2
				}
				set_technology = { improved_infantry_weapons = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = NEE_Streamline_Garand_Production
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = infantry_weapons
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mountain Unit (10th Light Infantry)
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.79
	title = new_england_events.79.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.79.d1
		trigger = {
			date < 1938.2.14
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.79.d2
		trigger = {
			date > 1938.2.13
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.79 option new_england_events.79.a"
		name = new_england_events.79.a
		army_experience = 10
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Alpine Infantry Division"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = mountaineers ICON = GFX_unit_mountaineers_icon_small COUNT = 10 }
				SUPPORT_1 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = recon ICON = GFX_unit_recon_icon_small }
				SUPPORT_2 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = engineer ICON = GFX_unit_engineer_icon_small }
				SUPPORT_3 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = artillery ICON = GFX_unit_artillery_icon_small }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Alpine Infantry Division" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Alpine Infantry Division" disband = yes } #no cheating
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Alpine Infantry Division"
				division_names_group = USA_MTN_01
				regiments = {
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					mountaineers = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					mountaineers = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 796 }
			limit = { valid_state_for_spawning_friendly_unit = yes }
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_spawn_unit
					TYPE = "Alpine Infantry Division"
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"10th Light Infantry\" division_template = \"Alpine Infantry Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Rebellion Events ###
country_event = { # The Yankee Rebellion
	id = new_england_events.80
	title = new_england_events.80.t
	desc = new_england_events.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			has_global_flag = { flag = CAN_seized_new_england days > 90 }
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = CAN_new_england_question
			NOT = { focus_progress = { focus = CAN_new_england_question progress > 0 } }
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion_over }
		NOT = { country_exists = NEE }
		any_state_in = {
			strategic_region = 186 #New England
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.80 option new_england_events.80.a"
		name = new_england_events.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_liberal_government = yes
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_WCA }
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = DEFAULT }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_new_england = yes }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_nee_resistance }
			add_to_variable = { var = global.CAN_yankee_rebellion value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = no }
				start_resistance = yes
			}
			add_resistance = 25
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england } } }
				add_compliance = -25
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { CAN_setup_NEE_suppression_decisions = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england }
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
			CAN = { USA_create_virginia_hall_operative = yes }
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.01
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.80 option new_england_events.80.b"
		name = new_england_events.80.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_WCA }
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = DEFAULT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA_spawn_new_england = yes
		NEE = {
			NEE_Starting_Great_Depression_Effect = yes
			#Popularities shifted to account for the rebellion
			hidden_effect = {
				set_popularities = {
					totalist = 0
					radical_socialist = 4
					syndicalist = 9
					social_democrat = 5
					social_liberal = 21
					market_liberal = 28
					social_conservative = 7
					authoritarian_democrat = 21

			930 = {

				force_enable_resistance = NEE

				set_compliance = 30
				set_resistance = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						has_country_flag = NEE_prepared_for_infil
					}
				}
				930 = {
					add_resistance = 30
					set_garrison_strength = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				930 = {
					add_resistance = 60

				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = new_england_events.88.a

			tag = NEE
		}
		add_war_support = -0.01
	}

	option = { # (WCA) - This should teach them!

		name = new_england_events.88.b

	}

### Rejoining the ACW Winner ###
country_event = { # New England receives request
	id = new_england_events.90
	title = new_england_events.90.t

	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.90.d.forced
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.90.d.choice
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold } }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = requester
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_elected_government = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = NEE_threshold
				value = 40
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_threshold
					value = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.90 option new_england_events.90.a"
		name = new_england_events.90.a #It seems we have no choice...
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = new_england_events.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.93 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.90 option new_england_events.90.b"
		name = new_england_events.90.b #We should reunite
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				add = -45
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 80 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = new_england_events.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.93 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.90 option new_england_events.90.c"
		name = new_england_events.90.c #Refuse
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_elected_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 45
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = CAN_refused_rejoin_usa
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.99 hours = 8 }
		}
	}
}

		name = new_england_events.97.c #then I guess we won't
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < 40 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_refused_rejoin_usa
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.20
		add_political_power = -100
		set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -10 }
		NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
		event_target:requester = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.99 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England has folded
	id = new_england_events.98
	title = new_england_events.98.t
	desc = new_england_events.98.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = NEE
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = event_target:requester
			has_war_with = NEE
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.98 option new_england_events.98.a"
		name = new_england_events.98.a
		set_global_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		annex_country = { target = NEE }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_new_england = yes }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_nee_resistance }
			add_to_variable = { var = global.CAN_yankee_rebellion value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = no }
				start_resistance = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { CAN_setup_NEE_suppression_decisions = yes }
		event_target:requester = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.99 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused to join
	id = new_england_events.99
	title = new_england_events.99.t

	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.99.d.exists
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.99.d.notexists
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = NEE
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 186
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					is_new_england = yes
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.99 option new_england_events.99.a"
		name = new_england_events.99.a #Then it's war!
		trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = event_target:war_country
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_elected_government = no
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.99 option new_england_events.99.b"
		name = new_england_events.99.b #We'll deal with this later
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { default_attack_AI_trigger = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England has joined anyhow
	id = new_england_events.100
	title = new_england_events.100.t
	desc = new_england_events.100.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = event_target:requester
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.100 option new_england_events.100.a"
		name = new_england_events.100.a #New England is ours!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = GBR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:requester
					ratio < 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:requester
					ratio < 1.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:requester
					ratio > 2.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_new_england = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.10
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:requester
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.100 option new_england_events.100.b"
		name = new_england_events.100.b #Let them have it
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		add_political_power = -100
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
				is_new_england = yes
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}

### Great Depression ###

country_event = { # Hidden Event to slowly reduce the Great Depression National Spirit
	id = new_england_events.101
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers #Maybe change this to something more accurate

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.101 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Great
		ai_chance = { base = 95 }
		# If at war, reduce effects faster
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_enemy_country = {
							is_neighbor_of = NEE
						}
					}
					enemies_strength_ratio > 0.6
				}
				else = {
					enemies_strength_ratio > 1
				}
				any_enemy_country = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_big = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_1
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_regular = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 3 }
			clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 7 }
				clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
				NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_regular = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		# If at peace, reduce effects slowly
		else = {
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_regular = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_gmbill_fails } }
			add_to_variable = { NEE_GWFaill_helper_var = 10 }
		}
	}

	option = { #HELPER for GWBill Failing
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.101 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Great
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_gmbill_fails }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = NEE.NEE_GWFaill_helper_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = { NEE_GWFaill_helper_var = 0 }
		# If at war, reduce effects faster
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_enemy_country = {
							is_neighbor_of = NEE
						}
					}
					enemies_strength_ratio > 0.6
				}
				else = {
					enemies_strength_ratio > 1
				}
				any_enemy_country = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_big = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_1
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_medium = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 3 }
			clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 7 }
				clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
				NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_medium = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		# If at peace, reduce effects slowly
		else = {
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_medium = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Fires of War - Removes Great Depression upon entrance into civil war
	id = new_england_events.102
	title = new_england_events.102.t
	desc = new_england_events.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = fires_of_war_fired
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.102 option new_england_events.102.a"
		name = new_england_events.102.a #Rally to the flag
		# Add flag
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = fires_of_war_fired }
		# Make the timer of the Great Depression rapidly decrease
		subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 20 }
		clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
		# Up a mobilization level
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation
					has_idea = war_economy
				}
			}
			increase_economic_mobilisation = yes
		}
		# Reduce stability while increasing war support
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}
}

country_event = { # Prepare to enter war
	id = new_england_events.104
	title = new_england_events.104.t
	desc = new_england_events.104.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.104 option new_england_events.104.a"
		name = new_england_events.104.a
		# Unlock Southern Fire
		# Check for ACC surrender in the independent path
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				CAN = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = CAN_supports_USA
					has_global_flag = CAN_supports_APG
					has_global_flag = CAN_supports_noone
				}
				ACC = {
					exists = yes
					surrender_progress > 0.05
				}
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.134
		}
	}
}

### Convincing CAN to back NEE in the 2ACW ###

# In the event that no one is backed - Begin to push for NEE as the Entente's best choice for winning the 2ACW
# If CAN backed another faction, they will decline NEE's request if the backed faction is winning (more powerful than the others combined)
# If CAN backed a faction that is currently losing, they are more likely to support

country_event = { # Reassess American Commitment
	id = new_england_events.123
	title = new_england_events.123.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.123.d.noone
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_noone
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.123.d.APG
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_APG
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.123.d.ACC
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_ACC
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.123.d.USA
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_USA
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_commons2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.123 option new_england_events.123.a"
		name = new_england_events.123.a # Decline NEE's terms
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_noone
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				WCA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.123 option new_england_events.123.b"
		name = new_england_events.123.b # APG is the better option
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_APG
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				APG = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.123 option new_england_events.123.c"
		name = new_england_events.123.c # ACC is the better option
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_ACC
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				ACC = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.123 option new_england_events.123.e"
		name = new_england_events.123.e # USA is the better option
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_USA
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				USA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				USA = {
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.123 option new_england_events.123.f"
		name = new_england_events.123.f # Agree to NEE's terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = { #If the ACW is already over, CAN should always decline
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
			}
			modifier = { #If the other tag is the Entente, CAN should decline this
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = APG
					is_in_faction_with = ACC
					is_in_faction_with = USA
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If fighting alongside another tag, don't bail on them
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war_together_with = APG
					has_war_together_with = ACC
					has_war_together_with = USA
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Don't support NEE if gamerule was set to only declare on WCA, or to never declare
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_NO }
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_WCA }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Don't support NEE if gamerule is set to support a specific side (unless they don't exist), or to support no one
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_NONE }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_USA }
						country_exists = USA
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_ACC }
						country_exists = ACC
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_APG }
						country_exists = APG
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				NOT = { NEE = { has_idea = NEE_limited_recognation1 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_GD_consumer_goods_var < 0.3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NEE = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NEE = {
					has_army_manpower = { size > 100000 }
				}
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.132
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					controls_all_owned_states = yes
					check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 49 }
					has_army_manpower = { size > 150000 }
					num_divisions > 20
					num_of_factories > 45
				}
				activate_decision = NEE_claim_usa_territory_harsh
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_USA }
				USA = { country_event = new_england_events.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_ACC }
				ACC = { country_event = new_england_events.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_APG }
				APG = { country_event = new_england_events.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAN }
				country_event = new_england_events.125 #Entente is informed of the two week pull out
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Reassess American Commitment - Repeatable until CAN says yes
	id = new_england_events.124
	title = new_england_events.124.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.124.d.noone
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_noone
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.124.d.APG
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_APG
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.124.d.ACC
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_ACC
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.124.d.USA
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_USA
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_commons1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.124 option new_england_events.124.a"
		name = new_england_events.124.a # Decline NEE's terms
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_noone
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				WCA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = new_england_events.133 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.124 option new_england_events.124.b"
		name = new_england_events.124.b # APG is the better option
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_APG
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				APG = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.124 option new_england_events.124.c"
		name = new_england_events.124.c # ACC is the better option
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_ACC
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				ACC = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.124 option new_england_events.124.e"
		name = new_england_events.124.e # USA is the better option
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_supports_USA
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				USA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				USA = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.133
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.124 option new_england_events.124.f"
		name = new_england_events.124.f # Agree to NEE's terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				NOT = { NEE = { has_idea = NEE_limited_recognation1 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_GD_consumer_goods_var < 0.3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NEE = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NEE = {
					has_army_manpower = { size > 100000 }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the other tag is the Entente, CAN should decline this
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = APG
					is_in_faction_with = ACC
					is_in_faction_with = USA
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Don't support NEE if gamerule was set to only declare on WCA, or to never declare
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_NO }
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_intervene option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_WCA }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Don't support NEE if gamerule is set to support a specific side (unless they don't exist), or to support no one
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_NONE }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_USA }
						USA = { exists = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_ACC }
						ACC = { exists = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_support option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_APG }
						APG = { exists = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = new_england_events.132
			clr_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					controls_all_owned_states = yes
					check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 49 }
					has_army_manpower = { size > 150000 }
					num_divisions > 20
					num_of_factories > 45
				}
				activate_decision = NEE_claim_usa_territory_harsh
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_USA }
				USA = { country_event = new_england_events.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_ACC }
				ACC = { country_event = new_england_events.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_APG }
				APG = { country_event = new_england_events.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAN }
				country_event = new_england_events.125 #Entente is informed of the two week pull out
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Entente fully wades into the 2ACW backing NEE's claim to be the legitimate America

country_event = { # Pulling the Entente out of the backed faction
	id = new_england_events.127
	title = new_england_events.127.t
	desc = new_england_events.127.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_watching

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.127 option new_england_events.127.a"
		name = new_england_events.127.a # Pull Entente Support Out
		# Clear CAN's support for other tags
		clr_global_flag = CAN_supports_noone
		clr_global_flag = CAN_supports_APG
		clr_global_flag = CAN_supports_ACC
		clr_global_flag = CAN_supports_USA

		# Remove ACW support idea
		# General Entente Idea
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_USA }
			remove_ideas = ACW_support_USA
			recall_volunteers_from = USA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_ACC }
			remove_ideas = ACW_support_ACC
			recall_volunteers_from = ACC
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_APG }
			remove_ideas = ACW_support_APG
			recall_volunteers_from = APG
		}
		# NEE specific
		if = {
			limit = { tag = NEE }
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = 10 }
			NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
		}
	}
}

				}
			}

				ACC = { has_war_with = USA }
				NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = prepare_for_war
						id = NEE
						value = -100
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ACC = { has_war_with = APG }
				NOT = { has_war_with = APG }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = ACC enemy = APG }
			hidden_effect = {
				APG = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = prepare_for_war
						id = NEE
						value = -100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.139 option new_england_events.139.b"
		name = new_england_events.139.b #Yay!
		trigger = {
			tag = ACC
		}

country_event = { #Provisional President
	id = new_england_events.200
	title = new_england_events.200.t
	desc = new_england_events.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress #Potentially grab a pic of the MA statehouse to use in the Election events

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ACC_Leader }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			end_coalition = yes
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.210 days = 16 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.160 days = 700 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.1550 days = 500 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.200 option new_england_events.200.a"
		name = new_england_events.200.a #The Republican Candidate - Barrows
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		promote_character = NEE_lewis_barrows
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_lewis_barrows = {
				add_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_provisional_president_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.152 days = 167 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.156 days = 234 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.200 option new_england_events.200.b"
		name = new_england_events.200.b #The Compromise Cabinet - Martin Jr.
		ai_chance = { base = 15 }
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		promote_character = NEE_joseph_martin_jr
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_joseph_martin_jr = {
				add_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_provisional_president_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_unity_cabinet_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NEE.coalition_stability = 0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.200 option new_england_events.200.c"
		name = new_england_events.200.c #The Democratic Candidate - Walsh
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		promote_character = NEE_david_walsh
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_david_walsh = {
				add_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_provisional_president_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = { #Restrict
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.217 option new_england_events.217.b"
		name = new_england_events.217.b
		# Add idea
		add_ideas = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2

country_event = { # Fair Labour 2 - Minimum Wage
	id = new_england_events.218
	title = new_england_events.218.t
	desc = new_england_events.218.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Child_Labor_Standard

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Enact
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.218 option new_england_events.218.a"
		name = new_england_events.218.a
		# Idea Swap
		if = { # Keep - Enact
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_3
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Restrict - Enact
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_5
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Reject this syndicalism!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.218 option new_england_events.218.b"
		name = new_england_events.218.b
		# Idea Swap
		if = { # Keep - Reject
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {  # Restrict - Reject
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_6
			}
		}
	}
}

### AALA Factory Events ###

country_event = { # [NEE] decide how many factories to send
	id = new_england_events.230
	title = new_england_events.230.t
	desc = new_england_events.230.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory_workers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
			has_war_with = APG
			has_war_with = WCA
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = ACC
		}
	}

	option = { # Send them 1 Factory
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.230 option new_england_events.230.a"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE.num_of_military_factories > 1 }
		}
		name = new_england_events.230.a
		# Give NEE a timed idea that removes [1] military factory for 90 days
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_1
			days = 90
		}
		army_experience = 5
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil = 1 }
		# Get the reverse variable as well
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = NEE_sent_mil }
		multiply_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = -1 }
		# Add the offmap mil to the backed country and
		# Send an event to the backed faction that they are receiving [1] NEE factory for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_factory_donation_tt_to_backed_faction_1 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Send them 2 Factories
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.230 option new_england_events.230.b"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE.num_of_military_factories > 5 }
		}
		name = new_england_events.230.b
		# Give NEE a timed idea that removes [2] military factory for 90 days
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
			days = 90
		}
		army_experience = 10
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil = 2 }
		# Get the reverse variable as well
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = NEE_sent_mil }
		multiply_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = -1 }
		# Add the offmap mils to the backed country and
		# Send an event to the backed faction that they are receiving [2] NEE factories for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_factory_donation_tt_to_backed_faction_2 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Send them 3 Factories
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.230 option new_england_events.230.c"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE.num_of_military_factories > 10 }
		}
		name = new_england_events.230.c
		# Give NEE a timed idea that removes [3] military factory for 90 days
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
			days = 90
		}
		army_experience = 15
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil = 3 }
		# Get the reverse variable as well
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = NEE_sent_mil }
		multiply_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = -1 }
		# Add the offmap mils to the backed country and
		# Send an event to the backed faction that they are receiving [3] NEE factories for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_factory_donation_tt_to_backed_faction_3 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Don't send anything
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.230 option new_england_events.230.e"
		name = new_england_events.230.e
		# Give NEE another event in 90 days to determine how many factories to send
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.230 days = 90 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # [FROM] is leasing us some war materiel
	id = new_england_events.231
	title = new_england_events.231.t
	desc = new_england_events.231.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory_workers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Like a good neighbour, NEE is there
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.231 option new_england_events.231.a"
		name = new_england_events.231.a
		# This will let the backed faction know that they are receiving factorie(s) from NEE for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
		# Give NEE another event in 90 days to determine how many factories to send
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.230 days = 90 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = new_england_events.250.a # Forgiveness is a virtue
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = 0.02
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WCA
				has_resistance = yes

			add_compliance = 5
		}

		add_stability = -0.02
	}

	after = {
		NEE_Political_Trial_Event_Queue = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Southern Racist 3 - Blow Over
	id = new_england_events.260
	title = new_england_events.260.t
	desc = new_england_events.260.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_red_summer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.260 option new_england_events.260.a"
		name = new_england_events.260.a # Get the lights on
		add_stability = -0.04
		add_political_power = -15
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 370 } # Mississippi
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = industrial_complex
					level > 1
				}
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = infrastructure
					level > 1
				}
			}
			damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 1.6 }
			damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 1.7 }
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 367 } # Alabama
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = industrial_complex
					level > 1
				}
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = infrastructure
					level > 1
				}
			}
			damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 1.1 }
			damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 1.9 }
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 365 } # Georgia
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = industrial_complex
					level > 1
				}
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = infrastructure
					level > 1
				}
			}
			damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 1.8 }

country_event = { # NEE requests land + NAP from CAN (CAN Event)
	id = new_england_events.300
	title = new_england_events.300.t
	desc = new_england_events.300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.300 option new_england_events.300.a"
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		name = new_england_events.300.a # Accept the deal
		# Friendship Modifier
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = NEE
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = NEE
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		# CAN and the Entente return American territory
		NEE_Returning_American_Land_effect_tt = yes
		# Mutual NAP to secure the Northern Border
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = NEE
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		NEE = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = CAN
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.300 option new_england_events.300.b"
		trigger = {
			ENT = { #Entente at war with the Internationale
				has_war_with = INT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				CAN = {
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = new_england_events.300.b
		add_political_power = -50
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE = { add_political_power = 50 }
		}
		# One way NAP from CAN
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = NEE
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		# Use this flag in the on_action for CAN vs ENG peace deal
		set_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { #Allow NEE to accept the promise or decline
				country_event = new_england_events.304
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #No. I don't think I will
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.300 option new_england_events.300.c"
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		name = new_england_events.300.c
		add_political_power = -100
		set_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
		NEE = { #Inform NEE that CAN is keeping the land
			country_event = new_england_events.304
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Partial or Total Denial of terms from the Buffalo Conference
	id = new_england_events.304
	title = new_england_events.304.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.304.d.return # Canada returns the territory they control
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.304.d.partial # Canada requests to keep the territory for the duration of the war
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.304.d.total # Total Rejection of return
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.304 option new_england_events.304.a"
		name = new_england_events.304.a # Allow the temporary loan
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		CAN = { clr_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory }
		add_political_power = 50
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.304 option new_england_events.304.b"
		name = new_england_events.304.b # This is unacceptable
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				add = 140
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = CAN ratio < 1.0 }
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
			}
		}
		CAN = { country_event = new_england_events.305 }
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.304 option new_england_events.304.c"
		name = new_england_events.304.c # Allow CAN to retain the territory
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				strength_ratio = { tag = CAN ratio > 2.0 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		CAN = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.304 option new_england_events.304.e"
		name = new_england_events.304.e # CAN returns the territory
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		NEE_Returning_American_Land = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
		CAN = { clr_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory }
	}
}

				add = 30

					has_government = radical_socialist #Edge case for non-TI soc MEX
					has_authdem_or_pataut_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_government = social_democrat
			}

		add_political_power = -100

			}

				add = 70
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist #Edge case for non-TI soc MEX
					has_government = radical_socialist #Edge case for non-TI soc MEX
					has_authdem_or_pataut_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist #Edge case for non-TI soc MEX
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_MEX_declines_terms_tt
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_country_flag = { flag = nee_mex_denies_terms days = 30 value = 1 }
		FROM = { country_event = new_england_events.311 }
	}
}

	title = new_england_events.309.t
	desc = new_england_events.309.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.309 option new_england_events.309.a"
		name = new_england_events.309.a # Offer them support if they reject terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				MEX = {
					OR = {
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				MEX = {
					has_government = totalist
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Add +25 if the ENT is gone
				add = 25
				NOT = {
					ENT = { exists = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Add +75 if GER is gone
				add = 75
				NOT = {
					GER = { exists = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		MEX = { set_country_flag = { flag = nee_int_supports_mex days = 30 value = 1 } }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.309 option new_england_events.309.b"
		name = new_england_events.309.b # Inform them that we cannot support them
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				MEX = { #MEX base chances
					OR = {
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						ENT = { exists = yes } #ENT still around
						GER = { exists = yes } #GER still standing
					}
				}
			}
		}
		MEX = { set_country_flag = { flag = nee_int_bails_on_mex days = 30 value = 1 } }
	}
	after = {
		MEX = { country_event = new_england_events.310 }
	}
}

	id = new_england_events.310
	title = new_england_events.310.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.310.d.mex_support
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = nee_int_supports_mex
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.310.d.mex_alone
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = nee_int_bails_on_mex
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.310 option new_england_events.310.a"
		name = new_england_events.310.a # Accept the American terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
			modifier = { # If a player INT chooses to support MEX's bid against America, AI MEX will never accept the American terms
				factor = 0
				INT = { is_ai = no }
				has_country_flag = nee_int_supports_mex
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 150
				has_country_flag = nee_int_bails_on_mex
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		NEE_MEX_Concessions = yes
		set_country_flag = { flag = nee_mex_agrees_terms days = 30 value = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.310 option new_england_events.310.b"
		name = new_england_events.310.b # Reject the American terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nee_int_bails_on_mex
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_MEX_declines_terms_tt
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_country_flag = { flag = nee_mex_denies_terms days = 30 value = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		NEE = { country_event = new_england_events.311 }
	}
}

			}

			target = MEX
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = {

			}

			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				strength_ratio = { tag = MEX ratio > 1.5 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}
