country_event = { #NEE invites us into the OAS
	id = new_england_events.316
	title = new_england_events.316.t
	desc = new_england_events.316.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.316 option new_england_events.316.a"
		name = new_england_events.316.a # Join
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = market_liberal }
				has_soccon_or_marlib_government = yes
			}
			modifier = { #CA countries are more likely to join if their neighbours are in the OAS. (Same with BRA URG and VEN)
				add = 20
				is_in_central_america = yes
				OR = {
					tag = BRA
					tag = URG
					tag = VEN
				}
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				tag = BRA
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		NEE = { set_country_flag = { flag = wishes_to_join_OAS value = 1 days = 15 } }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.316 option new_england_events.316.b"
		name = new_england_events.316.b # Decline
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = { # SA countries are less likely to join if their neighbours are in the OAS
				add = 20
				is_in_south_america = yes
				NOT = {
					tag = BRA
					tag = URG
					tag = VEN
				}
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				FROM = {
					is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					PAN = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					COS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					GUA = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					ELS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					HON = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					NIC = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				FROM = {
					is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 2
					PAN = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					COS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					GUA = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					ELS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					HON = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					NIC = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				FROM = {
					is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 4
					PAN = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					COS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					GUA = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					ELS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					HON = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					NIC = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = { has_government = market_liberal }
				has_soccon_or_marlib_government = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS
	}

	after = {
		NEE = { country_event = new_england_events.317 }
	}
}

country_event = { #FROM answers our invite to the OAS
	id = new_england_events.317
	title = new_england_events.317.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.317.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = wishes_to_join_OAS
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.317.d2
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.317 option new_england_events.317.a"
		name = new_england_events.317.a # Welcome!
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = wishes_to_join_OAS
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		else = { #Backup redundancy - NEE should never lose leadership of the OAS
			faction_leader = {
				add_to_faction = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.317 option new_england_events.317.b"
		name = new_england_events.317.b # Aw Shucks
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = -25
	}
}

country_event = { #NEE asks us to leave our faction
	id = new_england_events.318
	title = new_england_events.318.t
	desc = new_england_events.318.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.318 option new_england_events.318.a"
		name = new_england_events.318.a # Inform the faction head
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			overlord = { country_event = new_england_events.319 }
		}
		else = {
			faction_leader = { country_event = new_england_events.319 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #NEE requests we abandon FROM
	id = new_england_events.319
	title = new_england_events.319.t
	desc = new_england_events.319.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.319 option new_england_events.319.a"
		name = new_england_events.319.a # Drop them
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = { #If the American fleet is superior, reconsider our position abroad
				add = 3
				naval_strength_ratio = {
					tag = NEE
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the American army is superior, reconsider our position abroad
				add = 1
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = NEE
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the Americans have a direct border, this could be dicier
				add = 5
				FROM = {
					is_neighbor_of = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the Americans have a faction border, this could be dicier
				add = 1
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = NEE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				clear_all_relations = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			# Inform target country that they are being dropped from the faction
			set_country_flag = { flag = dropped_faction_member value = 1 days = 15 }
			country_event = new_england_events.321
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.319 option new_england_events.319.b"
		name = new_england_events.319.b # We support our friends
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				tag = INT
				GER = { exists = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				tag = GER
				INT = { exists = no }
				RUS = { exists = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				#check number of allied states in the western hemisphere
				set_temp_variable = { num = 0 }
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = THIS.faction_members
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = { is_in_central_america = yes }
							is_in_central_america = yes
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 2 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_central_america = yes }
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 1 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = { is_in_south_america = yes }
							is_in_south_america = yes
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 2 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_south_america = yes }
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 1 }
					}
				}
				add = num
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_OAS_declines_terms_tt
		FROM = { set_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction }
	}

	after = {
		NEE = { country_event = new_england_events.320 }
	}
}

# FROM.FROM in 320 refers to the country that NEE requested that they leave their European Faction
# FROM is the European Faction leader

country_event = { #NEE receives answer from European faction leader
	id = new_england_events.320
	title = {
		text = new_england_events.320.t1
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dropped_faction_member
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = new_england_events.320.t2
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = { has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.320.d1
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dropped_faction_member
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.320.d2
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = { has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.320 option new_england_events.320.a"
		name = new_england_events.320.a # Monroe upheld!
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dropped_faction_member
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 25
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		# Add 2nd level of tensions here
		FROM.FROM = {
			add_to_variable = {
				NEE_Tensions = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.320 option new_england_events.320.b"
		name = new_england_events.320.b # Don't push the issue
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 15 }
		FROM = { # Add one tension to the faction leader
			add_to_variable = {
				NEE_Tensions = 1
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		# Decrease opinion against faction leader
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		# FROM.FROM can stay in the faction!
		FROM.FROM = { country_event = new_england_events.322 }
		# FROM.FROM can stay in the faction! - Faction Leader
		FROM = { country_event = new_england_events.322 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.320 option new_england_events.320.c"
		name = new_england_events.320.c # This cannot stand
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0 #AI should never do this at first
			modifier = {
				#check tension level with faction leader
				set_temp_variable = { num = FROM.NEE_Tensions }
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					num = 10
				}
				add = num
			}
			modifier = { #If the European army is superior, reconsider war
				factor = 0.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the European fleet is superior, reconsider war
				factor = 0.25
				naval_strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM.FROM
		}
		# Faction informed about the war
		FROM.FROM = { country_event = new_england_events.323 }
		FROM = { country_event = new_england_events.323 }
	}
}

# Terms are as follows: CEN must dissolve into constituent states but are all welcome into the OAS

country_event = { #Dem CEN given terms
	id = new_england_events.327
	title = new_england_events.327.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.327.d1
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.327.d2
		trigger = {
			has_authoritarian_government = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.327 option new_england_events.327.a"
		name = new_england_events.327.a # We accept the terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = social_liberal }
				has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = market_liberal }
				has_soccon_or_marlib_government = yes
			}
			modifier = { #CA countries are more likely to join if their neighbours are in the OAS. (Same with BRA URG and VEN)
				add = 20
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 316 }
				release = COS
			}
			release = GUA
			release = NIC
			release = HON
			release = ELS
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 316 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = COS }
				release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
				COS = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative } }
				NEE = { add_to_faction = COS }
			}

			GUA_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GUA }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			GUA = { set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat } }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 311 }
				GUA = {
					transfer_state = 311
					add_state_claim = 311
				}
			}

			NIC_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NIC }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			NIC = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal } }

			HON_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HON }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			HON = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative } }

			ELS_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ELS }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			ELS = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal } }
		}
		NEE = {
			add_to_faction = GUA
			add_to_faction = NIC
			add_to_faction = HON
			add_to_faction = ELS
			set_country_flag = { flag = accepts_terms value = 1 days = 15 }
			country_event = new_england_events.328
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.327 option new_england_events.327.b"
		name = new_england_events.327.b # We decline the terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		set_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS
		NEE = {
			country_event = new_england_events.328
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #American Investors making moves in [FROM.GetNameDef]
	id = new_england_events.329
	title = new_england_events.329.t
	desc = new_england_events.329.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.329 option new_england_events.329.a"
		name = new_england_events.329.a # Embrace them
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_idea = NEE_Investments_idea
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { num = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { num = American_Investor_Influence }
				add = num
			}
		}
		# timed flag for description
		set_country_flag = { flag = allows_investors value = 1 days = 15 }
		# timed idea
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Investments_idea
			days = 100
		}
		# add to variable counter
		add_to_variable = {
			American_Investor_Influence = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					American_Investor_Influence > 2
				}
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.331 # People want to go free
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = new_england_events.330 # NEE told investors are allowed
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.329 option new_england_events.329.b"
		name = new_england_events.329.b # Throw them out
		ai_chance = { base = 4 }
		# add to variable counter
		add_to_variable = {
			American_Investor_Tension = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					American_Investor_Tension > 2
				}
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.331 # Investor Chaos
		}
		# timed flag for description
		set_country_flag = { flag = declines_investors value = 1 days = 15 }
		NEE = {
			country_event = new_england_events.330
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.336 option new_england_events.336.a"
		name = new_england_events.336.a # The right choice

			NOT = { has_event_target = declines_ultimatum }
		}

		add_political_power = 20
		FROM = { NEE_Form_Democracy_plus_OAS = yes }
		clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
	}

	option = {

			has_event_target = declines_ultimatum

		}
	}

		add_to_tech_sharing_group = nee_research

			NEE_Tensions = 1

			limit = {

				}
			}

		}

		}
	}

# Influence
country_event = { #Americans offer investments to entice us to join SFA
	id = new_england_events.372
	title = new_england_events.372.t
	desc = new_england_events.372.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.372 option new_england_events.372.a"
		name = new_england_events.372.a # We will allow them entry
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
			# Add modifier here to increase chances to join
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
		}
		# Bribe
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Investments_idea
			days = 180
		}
		# AI modifier
		add_to_variable = { NEE_Friendly = 2 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = allowed_SFA_influence days = 15 value = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.372 option new_england_events.372.b"
		name = new_england_events.372.b # Not interested right now
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			# Reduce the chances if target is authoritarian
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			# Less likely if in faction with Japan
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			NEE_Tensions = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NEE_Tensions > 4
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = hostile_tag_to_NEE
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = does_not_want_SFA_influence_temp days = 150 value = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.372 option new_england_events.372.c"
		name = new_england_events.372.c # Not interested ever
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = does_not_want_SFA_influence
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = new_england_events.373 }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.374.dnogea
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				941 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = GEA
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Kennedy

	trigger = {
		controls_state = 726
		has_war_with = JAP
		JAP = { has_navy_size = { size > 50 } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.374 option new_england_events.374.a"
		name = new_england_events.374.a # Hooray
		if = {
			limit = {
				941 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = GEA
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GEA
				modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kennedy_line_disgraced
			}
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.379 days = 187 random_days = 54 }
		}
	}
}

		text = new_england_events.380.d.default

			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
	}

						has_socialist_government = yes

							has_socialist_government = no

					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
		}

	}

			is_in_faction = yes

		}
		faction_leader = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.387 days = 2 } }

	option = { #We have no choice

			}
		}

	}

country_event = { #The Philippines rejoin America
	id = new_england_events.383
	title = new_england_events.383.t
	desc = new_england_events.383.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WIF_Palms

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FROM
			has_war_with = FROM.FROM #PHI's faction leader
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Excellent
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.383 option new_england_events.383.a"
		name = new_england_events.383.a
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				faction_leader = { save_event_target_as = former_faction_leader }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		}
		FROM = { get_current_government_type = yes }
		set_autonomy = {
			target = FROM
			autonomy_state = autonomous_puppet
			end_wars = no
		}
		FROM = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_elected_government = no }
				country_event = new_england_events.396
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = PHI_defied_faction_leader }
			event_target:former_faction_leader = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.385 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #America Demands the Return of the Philippines
	id = new_england_events.391
	title = new_england_events.391.t

	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.391.d.puppet_same_faction
		trigger = {
			has_subject = PHI
			is_in_faction_with = FROM
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.391.d.puppet
		trigger = {
			has_subject = PHI
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.391.d.annexed_same_faction
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 327
			is_in_faction_with = FROM
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.391.d.annexed
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 327
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_WIF_Palms

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Return the American lands
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.391 option new_england_events.391.a"
		name = new_england_events.391.a
		trigger = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { PHI = { is_subject = yes } }
				var:PHI.overlord = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PHI
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.392 days = 2 } }
	}

	option = { #No, we shall keep it
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.391 option new_england_events.391.b"
		name = new_england_events.391.b
		trigger = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.393 days = 2 } }
	}

	option = { #The Philippines aren't worth fighting over
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.391 option new_england_events.391.c"
		name = new_england_events.391.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -80
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { PHI = { is_subject = yes } }
				var:PHI.overlord = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PHI
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.392 days = 2 } }
	}

	option = { #The Philippines belong to us
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.391 option new_england_events.391.d"
		name = new_england_events.391.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 1 }
			}

				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 1.5 }
			}

				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio > 2 }
			}
		}

			ACC = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.404 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.403 option new_england_events.403.b"
		name = new_england_events.403.b
		trigger = {
			tag = ACC
		}
	}
}

# 410 - 1940 ACC led election

country_event = { # 1940 Presidential Election
	id = new_england_events.410
	title = new_england_events.410.t
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.410.d.normal #No Socdems
		trigger = { ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = no }
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.410.d.socdem #ACC allows Socdem if USA is dead
		trigger = { ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ACC_Olson_Roosevelt

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.209 days = 3 } } # Reset the congress mechanic for 1940
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = ACC
			has_country_flag = ACC_Leader
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.410 option new_england_events.410.a"
		name = new_england_events.410.a #Democrat - Olson
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_leader = { character = ACC_hiram_johnson }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_MARLIB }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCDEM }
						ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		promote_character = ACC_culbert_olson
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.410 option new_england_events.410.b"
		name = new_england_events.410.b #Republican - Roosevelt
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_MARLIB } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		promote_character = USA_quentin_roosevelt
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.410 option new_england_events.410.c"
		name = new_england_events.410.c #Farmer Labor - Wallace
		trigger = { ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCDEM } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		promote_character = ACC_henry_wallace
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = united_states_events.179 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = america_workers_congress_events.154 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

# 411-413 - 1944 ACC led election
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.411 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = ACC
			has_country_flag = ACC_Leader
		}
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election }
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.209 days = 3 } } # Reset the congress mechanic
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = ACC_culbert_olson }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.412 #Olson vs Langlie
		}
		else = {
			country_event = new_england_events.413 #Warren vs Downey
		}
	}
}

# 414-417 - 1948 ACC led election
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.414 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = ACC
			has_country_flag = ACC_Leader
		}
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election }
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = ACC_sheridan_downey }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.415 #Warren vs Downey
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = ACC_culbert_olson }
					has_country_leader = { character = ACC_earl_warren }
				}
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.416 #Martin vs Warren
		}
		else = {
			country_event = new_england_events.417 #Martin vs Langlie
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.417 option new_england_events.417.b"
		name = new_england_events.417.b #Republican - Langlie
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_country_leader = { character = ACC_arthur_langlie }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_MARLIB } }
			}
		}
		promote_character = ACC_arthur_langlie
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = ACC_clarence_martin
			promote_character = ACC_glen_taylor
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.417 option new_england_events.417.c"
		name = new_england_events.417.c #Farmer Labor - Taylor
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = ACC_philip_la_follette } }
			ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCDEM } }
			}
		}
		promote_character = ACC_glen_taylor
		ACC_farmer_labor_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = ACC_clarence_martin
			promote_character = ACC_arthur_langlie
			country_event = { id = united_states_events.180 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
			country_event = { id = united_states_events.181 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.417 option new_england_events.417.d"
		name = new_england_events.417.d #Farmer Labor - La Follette
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = ACC_philip_la_follette }
			ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCDEM } }
			}
		}
		ACC_farmer_labor_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = ACC_clarence_martin
			promote_character = ACC_arthur_langlie
		}
	}

# 418-421 - 1952 ACC led election
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.418 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = ACC
			has_country_flag = ACC_Leader
		}
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election }
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = ACC_clarence_martin }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.419 #Martin vs Cain
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = ACC_sheridan_downey }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.420 #Magnuson vs Cain
		}
		else = {
			country_event = new_england_events.421 #Magnuson vs Knowland
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Martin vs Cain
	id = new_england_events.419
	title = new_england_events.419.t

	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.419.d.ACC
		trigger = { ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.419.d.NEE
		trigger = { ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = no }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_ACC_Martin_Cain

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.419 option new_england_events.419.a"
		name = new_england_events.419.a #Democrat - Martin
		ai_chance = {
			base = 55
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ACC
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_MARLIB }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = ACC_path option = ACC_PATH_SOCDEM }
						ACC_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA_progressive_democrats_elected_effect = yes

			promote_character = ACC_harry_cain
		}

### Using Legitimacy Events ###

country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.441
	title = new_england_events.441.t
	desc = new_england_events.441.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_alufactory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept the contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.441 option new_england_events.441.a"
		name = new_england_events.441.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 30
		# Add negative idea for CAN
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_neg_infantry_contract_idea
			days = 90
		}
		# Event to NEE
		NEE = { set_country_flag = { flag = can_accepts_contract days = 15 value = 1 } }
	}

	option = { #We cannot accept
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.441 option new_england_events.441.b"
		name = new_england_events.441.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		NEE = { set_country_flag = { flag = can_declines_contract days = 15 value = 1 } }
	}

	after = {
		NEE = { country_event = new_england_events.442 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.442
	title = {
		text = new_england_events.442.t.accept
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_accepts_contract
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = new_england_events.442.t.decline
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_declines_contract
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.442.d.accept
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_accepts_contract
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = new_england_events.442.d.decline
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_declines_contract
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # ENT accepted the contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.442 option new_england_events.442.a"
		name = new_england_events.442.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_accepts_contract
		}
		# Add postive idea for NEE
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_pos_infantry_contract_idea
			days = 90
		}
		# Loss of legitimacy
		set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -15 }
		NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
	}

	option = { # ENT declined the contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.442 option new_england_events.442.b"
		name = new_england_events.442.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_declines_contract
		}
		# Refund
		add_political_power = 10
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.900
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.900 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a
		add_ideas = NEE_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		add_ideas = USA_civil_war_depression_idea
		add_ideas = USA_longist_resistance1
		set_country_flag = NEE_has_longist_terrorists
		add_ideas = USA_socialist_resistance1
		set_country_flag = NEE_has_syndicalist_terrorists
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		add_ideas = civilian_economy
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = NEE_Reorganise_National_Guard
				has_idea = selective_training_act
			}
			add_ideas = special_forces_focus
		}
		add_stability = -0.25
		add_war_support = -0.6
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ACC
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = new_england_events.400 days = 3 }
				ACC = { country_event = { id = new_england_events.400 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_government = market_liberal
		}
	}

			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy5

	is_triggered_only = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.461 option new_england_events.461.a"

			NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat = { is_dead = no }
		}

				add = 30
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}

			NEE_william_harriman = { set_character_flag = show_political_advisor_role }
		}
		activate_advisor = NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat_advisor
	}

			}
		}

## 500+ - Underground Railroad ##
# 500 - hidden LL
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.500
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.500 option 1"
		if = { #If downstream is closed, no missions
			limit = {
				261 = { has_state_flag = blocked_route } #Ohio
			}
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.500 days = 45 }
		}
		else_if = { #If Michigan is closed, furthest mission is Ohio
			limit = {
				393 = { has_state_flag = blocked_route } #Michigan
			}
			activate_mission = NEE_LL_Ohio_Albany_Route
		}
		else_if = { #If Minnesota is closed, furthest mission is Michigan
			limit = {
				391 = { has_state_flag = blocked_route } #Minnesota
			}
			activate_mission = NEE_LL_Michigan_Ohio_Route
		}
		else = { #Full Mission
			activate_mission = NEE_LL_Minnesota_Michigan_Route
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.505 option new_england_events.505.a"
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		name = new_england_events.505.a
		event_target:UR_state = { set_state_flag = helped_parallel_group }
		# Add partial patrol
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:UR_state = { has_state_flag = completed_smuggle_group } }
			event_target:UR_state = { clr_state_flag = completed_smuggle_group }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NEE_LL_people_army = 35 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NEE_LL_people_civ = 35 }
			NEE = { NEE_LL_Success = yes }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = {
				NEE.LL_people_route = 35
				tooltip = NEE_LL_increase_population
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.505 option new_england_events.505.b"
		name = new_england_events.505.b
		trigger = {
			event_target:UR_state = { has_state_flag = completed_smuggle_group }
		}

	}

### 1940 elections ###
country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.600 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ACC_Leader
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		}
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.209 days = 3 } # Reset the congress mechanic
		}
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_lewis_barrows }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.601 #Hurley vs Barrows
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_david_walsh }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.602 #Walsh vs Winant
		}
		else = {
			country_event = new_england_events.603 #Hurley vs Winant
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hurley vs Barrows
	id = new_england_events.601
	title = new_england_events.601.t
	desc = new_england_events.601.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Hurley_Barrows

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Democrat - Hurley
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.601 option new_england_events.601.a"
		name = new_england_events.601.a
		ai_chance = { base = 55 }
		promote_character = NEE_charles_hurley
		USA_progressive_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican - Barrows
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.601 option new_england_events.601.b"
		name = new_england_events.601.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_lewis_barrows = {
				remove_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NEE_charles_hurley
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.162 days = 635 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Walsh vs Winant
	id = new_england_events.602
	title = new_england_events.602.t
	desc = new_england_events.602.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Walsh_Winant

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Democrat - Walsh
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.602 option new_england_events.602.a"
		name = new_england_events.602.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }

		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_david_walsh = {
				remove_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NEE_john_winant
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.166 days = 305 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.219 days = 800 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican - Winant
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.602 option new_england_events.602.b"
		name = new_england_events.602.b
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		promote_character = NEE_john_winant
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.163 days = 176 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.164 days = 394 }
			country_event = { id = new_england_events.183 days = 1100 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.611 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ACC_Leader
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election
		}
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_george_aiken }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.612 #Bowles vs Aiken
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_william_harriman }
			}
			country_event = new_england_events.613 #Harriman vs Dewey
		}
		else = {
			country_event = new_england_events.614 #Bowles vs Dewey
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Bowles vs Aiken
	id = new_england_events.612
	title = new_england_events.612.t
	desc = new_england_events.612.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Bowles_Aiken

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Democrat - Bowles
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.612 option new_england_events.612.a"
		name = new_england_events.612.a
		promote_character = NEE_chester_bowles
		USA_progressive_democrats_elected_effect = yes
	}

	option = { # Republican - Aiken
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event new_england_events.612 option new_england_events.612.b"
		name = new_england_events.612.b
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NEE_chester_bowles
		}
	}
}

}

country_event = {
	id = new_england_events.1000 #system event to add NEE's debuffs if they get the mainland after the ACW has ended (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CAN
			has_war_with = MEX
			country_exists = WCA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = APG
			has_country_flag = already_got_acw_debuffs
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = ACC }
			is_in_faction_with = ACC
		}
	}

	option = {
		country_event = american_civil_war_events.24
	}
}
